-- obfuscated @ discord.gg/25ms, obfuscation: ib2 fork
return(function(...)local C,A,R=table,string,bit local D,P,O,S,N,g,W,V,Q,e,d=A.byte,A.char,A.sub,C.concat,C.insert,math.ldexp,getfenv and getfenv()or _ENV,setmetatable,select,unpack or
